Battle Royale State of Development V4","content":"<h2>Service Stability Issues</h2>\nWe were not able to stay ahead of our continued growth and multiple of our backend services have been struggling under load the last several weeks (e.g. friends functionality and general login service). And we also shipped v2.3.0 with significant bugs.<br />\n<br />\nWe don’t consider either acceptable. We have changed our release plans & processes to help improve quality of client builds, and scrambled people to make traction on backend scalability by any means possible.\n<h2><br />\nOngoing Optimizations</h2>\nWhen you play some Battle Royale, we want the time from when you’re in the lobby to when you’re in the action to be as short as possible. We’re continuing to work on load time improvements to help with that. You want a smoother in-game experience, and we agree!<br />\n<br />\nWe are testing and bug fixing  improvements that will deliver better level streaming with less hitches. We’re getting close to being able to test a significant optimization to our networking code that should get us closer to running the server at a solid 20 Hz even in the beginning of the match.\n<h2><br />\n60 FPS on Console</h2>\nLater this month we plan to add an optional 60 FPS mode for Battle Royale on consoles (PS4, PS4 Pro, Xbox One, Xbox One X). This 60 FPS mode is tuned for each console to maximize frame rate while minimizing loss of visual quality. \n\n<h2><br />\nWest Coast (US) / Brazilian Servers</h2>\nWe feel your pain with ping (our internal playtests are done across the ocean). We have added West Coast and will add Brazilian Xbox servers to provide better connection options.<br />\n<br />\n<em>The below picture shows average ping improvements for West Coast (US)</em><br />\n<br />\n<img alt=\"west-coast-servers-ping.PNG\" height=\"auto\" src=\"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Ffortnite-battle-royale-state-of-development-v4%2Fwest-coast-servers-ping-1600x958-0c685f1ef67f09659fdb2b8cfa151cefefd675c5.PNG\" width=\"auto\" /><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n \n<h2>Matchmaking Improvements</h2>\nWe are working on changes to matchmaking that are aimed at creating matches with a more balanced distribution of skill.\n\n<h2><br />\nArt</h2>\nThe Art team has been having a blast coming up with cool ideas for cosmetics in Fortnite Battle Royale. Since the holiday event we’ve enjoyed seeing the community embrace outfits like the Fort Knights and Disco Heroes.That trend towards more adventurous items will continue.<br />\n<br />\nGliders deserve love too and we’ve begun work on a pipeline that allows us to add new model parts and materials to create more unique Gliders. Here is an example that might pop into the store in the near future!<br />\n<br />\n<img alt=\"ConceptArt_DragonGlider.jpg\" height=\"auto\" src=\"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Ffortnite-battle-royale-state-of-development-v4%2FConceptArt_DragonGlider-1920x1080-baeee883e957ee0b466676b746a8caff5c0aa2c0.jpg\" width=\"auto\" /><br />\n<br />\nAdditionally, we are working on new Outfits that change more of the model, similar to how we created Raptor!<br />\n<br />\n<img alt=\"ConceptArt_SpaceSquadFemale.jpg\" height=\"auto\" src=\"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Ffortnite-battle-royale-state-of-development-v4%2FConceptArt_SpaceSquadFemale-1920x1080-95711eec4095b8030c5b5f9f3fe163e64c0a00e3.jpg\" width=\"auto\" /><br />\n<br />\nWe want to hear from you! We love your ideas, and thanks to reddit user /u/Pandanapper the Llama Unicorn Pickaxe for the Brite Bomber has come to life!<br />\n<br />\n<img alt=\"ConceptArt_BriteBomberPickaxe.jpg\" height=\"auto\" src=\"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Ffortnite-battle-royale-state-of-development-v4%2FConceptArt_BriteBomberPickaxe-1920x1080-95a0a802612be0085e78078a32cc66cfacdaf5e2.jpg\" width=\"auto\" /><br />\n<br />\nHow about making the things you already own even better? We’re looking at previously released cosmetic items and finding ways to juice them up! One example is adding new visual effects to the Party Animal Pickaxe (now with splashing animations).\n<div class=\"embed-responsive embed-responsive-16by9\"><iframe class=\"embed-responsive-item\" frameborder=\"0\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/SrIHSjbmMoA\" width=\"100%\"></iframe><br />\n<br />\nGameplay</div>\nWeekly updates, items, and features!<br />\n<br />\nWe’re continuing to prototype new weapons and consumables, and will roll them out as they’re ready. Additionally, we’re looking to add different types of items down the road (beyond just weapons and consumables) that will allow for exciting new ways to play.<br />\nNext week we’ll be putting our first weapon (SMG) into the Vault. These weapons may or may not return and this allows us to manage the weapon pool as we introduce newer weapons.<br />\n<br />\nYou have also helped to surface quality of life fixes, and here are some on the short list right now are:\n<ul style=\"margin-left: 40px;\">\n\t<li>Improved building controls on console</li>\n\t<li>Team Communication outside of voice chat</li>\n\t<li>Ability to re-queue from the death screen</li>\n\t<li>Ability to preemptively hold down the search button while approaching a searchable object</li>\n\t<li>Display of how much ammo is loaded into a gun on the weapon widget</li>\n\t<li>Larger map w/ zoom</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3><em>Quickbar Improvements</em></h3>\nWe’ve been working on making that swap between your weapon bar and your build bar feel more crisp. Making it easier to swap between build pieces when you have moderate ping and removing visual stuttering when you quickly scroll through items are being worked on as well!\n\n<h2><br />\nSocial</h2>\nMany of you love playing Fortnite with friends. We take that to heart so we’ve been in the lab cooking up ways to improve that. In the short term we’ll enhance your abilities to find and play with your friends. Long term we plan to rework the social architecture and all social features within Fortnite (i.e. chat and friends list).<br />\n<br />\nInvite your friends, first from Facebook (PC first, console to follow), soon with other social networks! We’re also working on a “Looking for Group” feature to make it easier for your squad to party up or look for more!<br />\n<br />\n<img alt=\"2018-02-07-11_35_59-Fortnite.png\" height=\"auto\" src=\"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Ffortnite-battle-royale-state-of-development-v4%2F2018-02-07-11_35_59-Fortnite-1600x900-ecff25436212963dae7aec7970f858c27e26e242.png\" width=\"auto\" /><br />\n<br />\nFeature Example: You’ll be able to spectate and chat with your friends while you wait for them to finish up that solo match, in-game!<br />\n<br />\nIf you’re feeling generous, we have a feature on the horizon just for you ;)\n<h2><br />\nLimited Time Modes</h2>\nWe’ve been hammering away at Limited Time Modes! Getting you multiple playlists (solo, duo and squads) during LTMs is at the top of the priority stack. We’ve been using multiple data points (including your feedback) to iterate our existing LTM’s and to build brand new LTM’s. We are planning to quickly spin up a dozen or so LTMs, some of these may be more straightforward (e.g. along the lines of Sniper Shootout, Sneaky Silencer etc.). We also use LTMs to test new Shooting Models.<br />\n<br />\nFrom there, we want to make internal improvements so we can introduce more involved LTMs (e.g. “floor is lava”).<br />\n<br />\nModes we plan to run in the next month or so:\n<ul>\n\t<li>Blitz Mode (shorter matches!)</li>\n\t<li>Drop into the first circle</li>\n\t<li>Generally less time between circles</li>\n\t<li>Team sizes in between 50v50 and squads</li>\n\t<li>50v50 v2\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Closer to the <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sZcuF1T4Vxw\">50v50 Trailer experience</a></li>\n\t\t<li>Split to start</li>\n\t\t<li>Converge on Battle</li>\n\t\t<li>Bus for each team</li>\n\t\t<li>See all your squadmates on the map</li>\n\t\t<li>More supply drops</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2><br />\nCustom Matches</h2>\nYou may have seen some players getting involved in our Fortnite Friendlies, which is our way of testing out private match functionality and working out the bugs. We want to iron out some of the bigger kinks before rolling this out to the entire game!<br />\n \n<h2>Audio</h2>\n<strong>Footsteps</strong><br />\nAbove/below footsteps have been implemented, meaning that different audio assets will play depending on another player’s position relative to you. These assets have been filtered based on real-world data to sound like they’re on the floor above you versus the floor below you.<br />\n<br />\nIn addition, we also remove some of the filtered above/below content if there’s direct line of sight between you and the other player. This “opens” the footsteps up a bit and helps in cases where the building gets a little wild.<br />\n<br />\n<strong>Listener Position</strong><br />\nWe’ll be changing the way the listener behaves for 2.5. Volume attenuation will be moved to the player’s location, and panning will still be calculated from the camera. Previously, panning and volume attenuation were based on the camera’s location. This led to a lot of confusion when moving the camera around to locate a chest, as the volume would dip in and out as the camera swung around.<br />\n<br />\n<strong>Building</strong><br />\nAudio for placing structures has been redesigned to put more emphasis on the “placement” of structures. So if a player is rapidly approaching you and building ramps up to your tower, you’ll hear a steady “chunk, chunk, chunk” as they place the structures, extending to about the range of sprinting footsteps. We’ll be closely monitoring how this affects building, both in offensive and defensive situations.\n<h2><br />\nBattle Pass Season 3</h2>\nWe thank all of you for your support throughout Season 2. We’re excited and can’t wait to announce details on the Battle Pass for Season 3!<br />\nFor example, we heard your concerns about the daily challenge system.<br />\n<br />\nIn Season 3  we’re adding flexibility by replacing the second daily challenge with a new weekly system. Battle Pass owners will unlock a new bundle of quests each week of the season which can be completed any time before the end of the season.<br />\n \n<h2> </h2>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br Back then, we stated two goals for our combat:</p>\n\n<ul dir=\"ltr\" style=\"margin-left: 40px;\">\n\t<li>Goal #1 – Pistol sniping at long range should not be possible.</li>\n\t<li>Goal #2 – Our weapons should have characteristics that encourage a wide range of engagements based on: distance to target, target type, ammo availability, etc.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\">One of our favorite things about Fortnite Battle Royale is choosing how to engage another player - whether that’s building cover and closing the gap, dropping from above, sneaking around, or just going in guns blazing. Unfortunately, it can be frustrating when those plans are disrupted by a shot that randomly misses your target.</p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\">To attempt to address this concern, we’ve been prototyping a few different approaches to the shooting model. Those prototypes include:</p>\n\n<ol dir=\"ltr\" style=\"margin-left: 40px;\">\n\t<li>First-Shot Accuracy</li>\n\t<li>Perfect Accuracy + Recoil (Note: Some of you might’ve seen videos online - an early version was accidentally turned on a while back. Oops!)</li>\n</ol>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\">The first prototype we’re ready to test is First-Shot Accuracy, and in many ways this version is very similar to our current experience. However, there are a few changes:</p>\n\n<ul style=\"margin-left: 40px;\">\n\t<li><strong>Weapons now have first-shot accuracy, indicated by a red glow on the reticle. This is applied when:</strong>\n\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Standing still</li>\n\t\t<li>Aiming (not hip-firing)</li>\n\t\t<li>Aim spread is at peak accuracy (Basically, if you haven’t fired recently. It is different per weapon)</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li><strong>Headshot critical hits have been reduced</strong>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Shotguns are now 150% damage (was 250%).</li>\n\t\t<li>All other weapons with headshot crits are now 200% damage (was 250%).</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li><strong>Damage fall-off has been introduced for some weapons</strong>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Damage applies at 100% to a fixed range.</li>\n\t\t<li>Fall-off begins at different ranges (depending on the weapon), and decreases to 70% damage.</li>\n\t\t<li>Sniper Rifles, Rocket/Grenade Launchers, and Shotguns are unaffected.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li><strong>Other balance adjustments</strong>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Semi-Auto Sniper has had its damage increased to 75/78 (from 63/66).</li>\n\t\t<li>Scoped Assault Rifle has had its damage increased to 25/26 (from 23/24).</li>\n\t\t<li>+2 Base damage to all SMGs.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\">Everyone should feel encouraged to give this test a try - wins and other stats will count while playing this mode.</p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\">Our intent is to run multiple shooting tests, and we’ll be gathering data from many different sources (internal analytics, community sentiment, and various social platforms). Your participation is key! We want to be confident that what we have is better for the community, across all platforms and skill levels.</p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\"> </p>\n","featured":false,"date":"2018-02-02T18:43:41.871Z","link":"b355d485-277a-4473-b640-a93742edd16b","_id":"b355d485-277a-4473-b640-a93742edd16b","pageMapping":"b355d485-277a-4473-b640-a93742edd16b","slug":"shooting-test-1","urlPattern":"/zh-HK/blog/shooting-test-1","locale":"zh-HK","_script":"undefined","category":["announcements"],"tags":[],"catLocaleMap":{},"nextSlug":"v-2-4-2-patch-notes","prevSlug":"v-2-4-0-patch-notes"},{"trending":false,"noTopImage":false,"image":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fv-2-4-0-patch-notes%2FFN_Blog_Cozy-Campfire_1920x480-1920x480-b1601084a0ee00f6ac4d7f9952e7b782e41dc93d.jpg","author":"The Fortnite Team","enableLightbox":false,"_type":"Common Post","shareImage":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fv-2-4-0-patch-notes%2FES_FNBR_Social_MiniGun-600x600-f4bddde2e9482f63b35dd32a590318fb96c010cc.jpg","title":"V.2.4.0 Patch Notes","content":"<div dir=\"ltr\">\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><strong>UPDATE</strong>: The V.2.4.0 patch is now live!</p>\n</div>\n\n<div dir=\"ltr\">Hey Fortnite players,</div>\n\n<p>You’ve probably run into a few issues playing Fortnite this past week. increasing the audio volume if you’re aiming at them.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Removed the static audio from living room televisions.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li emotes.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"color:#b83df2;\">World</span></h2>\n\n<div dir=\"ltr\"><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></div>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div The damage area was previously too large.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue which prevented the Shield Potion and Slurp Juice visual effects from playing when the player is already shielded.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue that made Cozy Campfires appear to be active after they have expired.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue which caused collision of eliminated players to persist for too long.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue which allowed players to hide inside of supply drops if the supply drop landed on a crouched player.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue which allowed players to pass through walls as they edited them.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Optimized the speed at which players can cycle building pieces under poor network conditions.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue which caused dropped items to fall off the edge of the map and spawn near a living player.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Kicking a basketball through a soccer net no longer counts as a goal. Soccer balls still count.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"color:#b83df2;\">Weapons</span></h2>\n\n<div dir=\"ltr\"><strong><em>Bug Fixes</em></strong></div>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Improved the accuracy of grenade arcs.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue which allowed players to switch between two scoped weapons without leaving the scoped view.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Player&#39;s weapons will no longer disappear for a short time after the effects of the Boogie Bomb wear off.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Reduced the delay between throwing a grenade and switching to another weapon.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"color:#b83df2;\">General</span></h2>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Shadowplay Highlights now records player knockdowns (DBNO).</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li>Quitting a match early will no longer award stat or challenge progress. Progress will only be awarded when a player leaves after they are eliminated or have won.</li>\n\t<li>Players in NA region can now choose between East and West coast servers. Full details <a href=\"https://www.epicgames.com/fortnite/forums/news/announcements/146075-v-2-3-0-server-update-na-west-east-coast-servers\">here.</a></li>\n</ul>\n<em><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></em>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Players can no longer purchase the Battle Pass x10 Tier bundle when at or above Battle Pass tier 65.</div>\n\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">We fixed this on January 19th and affected players have been compensated.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue which allowed items in the locker to rotate on the wrong axis while spinning them.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue which caused the client to lock up after ALT-TABing on PC.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">While spectating, players will now be returned to scoped view when the spectated player switches between scoped weapons, instead of being pulled into third-person view.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Brick building effects have been fixed.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Players can now mute party members from the lobby screen.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Players banned from voice chat can no longer use it on the lobby screen.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"color:#b83df2;\">UI</span></h2>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Added Auto Decline Friend Requests as a new option for PC players to the Social Widget.</div>\n\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">When enabled, friend requests will be auto-declined. Enabling this option will decline all pending friend requests.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<div dir=\"ltr\"><em><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></em></div>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Friend and Party invite notifications will now correctly appear for Battle Royale players that have never played Save the World.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">You no longer open the fullscreen map while spectating a player with report menu up,</div>\n\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">This issue only occurred if a player was using the “Combat Pro” controller config.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">The radial emote menu will no longer persist after the warm-up phase if left open.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Characters pose no longer resets after opening the news widget.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">The ping value displayed in the Net Debug Stats UI is now more accurate. the World</h1>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"color:#b83df2;\">Mutant Storm Event Returns!</span></h2>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">This storm season, Mutant Storms will appear in greater numbers.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Mutant Storm mission alerts award Storm Tickets in addition to the Evolution Materials that they usually drop.</div>\n\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Quota: 10 per day.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Up to 5 Mutant Storms are available at a time in Stonewood, and up to 25 Active Storms are available at a time in Plankerton, Canny Valley, and Twine Peaks.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Purchased upgrade Llamas award Storm Tickets.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li>All missions will continue to award Seasonal Gold, and Daily Quests will continue to award Daily Coins.\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Seasonal Gold will reset once the Spring Event Or just check out all the bug fixes in the V.2.3.0 Patch Notes!","featured":false,"date":"2018-01-24T10:46:00.000Z","link":"e0279c38-f74e-4bbd-9705-d843ecb7772e","_id":"e0279c38-f74e-4bbd-9705-d843ecb7772e","pageMapping":"e0279c38-f74e-4bbd-9705-d843ecb7772e","slug":"v-2-3-0-patch-notes","urlPattern":"/zh-HK/blog/v-2-3-0-patch-notes","locale":"zh-HK","_script":"undefined","category":["patch notes"],"tags":[],"catLocaleMap":{},"nextSlug":"v-2-4-0-patch-notes","prevSlug":"dev-deep-dive-map-update"},{"trending":false,"noTopImage":false,"image":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fv-2-2-0-patch-notes%2FRaptorSkinScreenshot-%281%29_770x433_1516246998866-770x433-abbd90b778916d3509b8d03df14cfac0042669aa.png","author":"The Fortnite Team","enableLightbox":false,"_type":"Common Post","shareImage":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2FtempUpload%2FMapUpdateScreenshot005-4304x2422-f0fe733f5772400b3292e5a0aa55225a8f7f5507.png","title":"Dev Deep Dive: Map Update","content":"<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;white-space:pre;\">Excited for the new map update this week? Get a dev perspective with some of the Fortnite team! </span></p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><em><span style=\"font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;white-space:pre;\">David Spalinski, Lead Level Designer:</span></em></p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><em><span style=\"font-size:13px;\">Since the initial release of Battle Royale in September we’ve been keeping an eye on opportunities to improve and add to the map. We had some initial predictions about what would make it better for you, but chose to take the time to watch, listen, and play with the community to learn about various things we couldn’t have known at the onset. We’ve taken that knowledge and built it into this update, which represents a major iteration on the Battle Royale map.</span></em></p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><em><span style=\"font-size:13px;\">One of the primary things we identified needed improvement was the density of the points of interests (POIs) on the western side of the map. The density on the eastern side has offered a good pacing for loot, traversal, and combat engagement frequency, so we wanted to bring some of that to the western side. As a result, many new POIs have been added west of the river, each with their own identity.</span></em></p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><em><span style=\"font-size:13px;\">Tilted Towers is a city located just south of Loot Lake, which adds a hotspot close to the center of the map. It offers a fair amount of vertical gameplay through taller buildings that players can land on, fight through, or even defend against other nearby fortified buildings. When constructing this POI, we wanted to create something on the larger end of the scale, similar in size to Pleasant Park or Retail Row. We targeted it as a place where many players could choose to land, and still be able to get enough weapons to be able to hold their own.</span></em></p>\n</blockquote>\n \n\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><em><span style=\"font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;white-space:pre;\">Sidney Rauchberger, Lead Level Designer:</span></em></p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-size:13px;\"><em>Another point of interest just west of the river is an underground mine called Shifty Shafts. Unlike the heights of the buildings in Tilted Towers, this POI is all about tighter underground tunnels, which present opportunities to sneak up on or flank your opposition. From the beginning we thought that the idea of adding a mine just sounded fun, and now we’ve been able get one in there.  This location is one to be explored, not scouted from a distance, since all of the good loot is on the inside.</em></span></p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-size:13px;\"><em>Snobby Shores is a private residential neighborhood on the west coast of the island made up of multiple fenced houses. By fencing in the houses, they act as self-contained combat areas, allowing for intimate combat engagements that are focused on the immediate surroundings. Additionally, the housing plots are arranged in a line, which organizes and brings clarity to the combat relationship from house to neighboring house.</em></span></p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-size:13px;\"><em>When identifying which specific areas of the map were under utilized, the northwest was near the top of the list. Beyond visiting Pleasant Park or being forced there by the storm, there wasn’t much of a draw to go there. As a result, we’ve added Junk Junction. This point of interest is a junkyard full of crushed cars stacked upon each other. We took care to ensure that among this junk you would be free to build around it, or jump from pile to pile without a need for building. This offers player’s flexibility in how they want to pursue their opponents or loot.</em></span></p>\n</blockquote>\n \n\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><em><span style=\"font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;white-space:pre;\">Stuart Fitzsimmons, Senior Level Designer:</span></em></p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-size:13px;\"><em>Separate from the new POIs, we also wanted to add visual variety to larger sections of the map. To accomplish this, the map is now divided into four biomes. The grassland has a similar look to what you’ve come to expect from the map until now, but the swamp, farmland, and mountain areas bring their own visual identity. This is mostly done with changes in color tones evident on the terrain, as well as different looking trees & vegetation. To accomplish this, we reworked the core of how the terrain is computed for display, making it more flexible in order to add these biomes. Beyond adding visual variety, the idea behind this was to allow players to associate where they are on the island with the look of the environment surrounding them. You’ll be able to easily spot these biomes from the battle bus or when bringing up the map.</em></span></p>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"font-size:13px;\"><em>We’re looking forward to seeing how players adapt their strategies as a result of the changes and additions present in this map update. We’re hoping you will find a new favorite place to land, route to take, or building to fortify during the end game. We’ll be continuing to watch, listen, and play with everyone to identify ways to improve upon the map from here, and look forward to your feedback.</em></span></p>\n</blockquote>\n  ","trendingImage":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2FtempUpload%2FMapUpdateScreenshot005-4304x2422-f0fe733f5772400b3292e5a0aa55225a8f7f5507.png","cat":"Announcements","sticky":false,"short":"Take a deeper dive into the Map Update with a few of our Fortnite Devs, as they share some of their favorite new spots!","featured":false,"date":"2018-01-18T17:00:00.000Z","link":"f96a035e-d004-4b01-b199-7ceaf6d9e791","_id":"f96a035e-d004-4b01-b199-7ceaf6d9e791","pageMapping":"f96a035e-d004-4b01-b199-7ceaf6d9e791","slug":"dev-deep-dive-map-update","urlPattern":"/zh-HK/blog/dev-deep-dive-map-update","locale":"zh-HK","_script":"undefined","category":["announcements"],"tags":[],"catLocaleMap":{},"nextSlug":"v-2-3-0-patch-notes","prevSlug":"v-2-2-0-patch-notes"},{"trending":false,"noTopImage":false,"image":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fv-2-2-0-patch-notes%2FNewsFeed_Header-1920x480-8b2b6b63dd6173c9c9aa7d8b98ed31fe642838bc.jpg","author":"The Fortnite Team","enableLightbox":false,"_type":"Common Post","shareImage":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2FtempUpload%2FMapUpdateScreenshot005-4304x2422-f0fe733f5772400b3292e5a0aa55225a8f7f5507.png","title":"V.2.2.0 Patch Notes","content":"<div dir=\"ltr\"><em>Patch V.2.2.0 is planned to release January 18. forward and backward while gliding when facing straight up and down.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">The Cozy Campfire trap no longer heals eliminated players.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue which caused the glider to sometimes deploy sideways after using a launchpad.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"color:#b83df2;\">World</span></h2>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">The map has been updated with many new points of interest, biomes, and more!</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Players now interact with grass and foliage as they walk through it.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Added water effects when entering and exiting water.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Added a new post-process effect for when your camera goes below the water surface.</div>\n\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">It will now look like you are actually underwater, and you can no longer see for an infinite distance.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Added Ammo Boxes to Dusty Depot.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Increased the amount of metal harvested from shipping containers.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<div dir=\"ltr\"><em><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></em></div>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Water no longer blocks bullets and projectiles.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"color:#b83df2;\">Item Shop</span></h2>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Additional flexibility has been added to the store. This allows us to display more featured and daily items in the future.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Starting on January 21st, 2018 the Weekly Item shop is changing to the Featured Item Shop.</div>\n\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Offers will update twice weekly instead of once.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">When spectating a far away player, a “loading” message may be displayed for a short time, and the game world will appear after loading completes.  You cannot switch to another spectated player until the load completes.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">The \"Reset Building Choice\" option now defaults to \"Off\" in Battle style=\"color:#b83df2;\">Performance</span></h2>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Added level streaming, which loads the world on-the-fly as you move around, enabling a richer map and improved performance.</div>\n\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Improved frame rate by greatly reducing the number of objects that need to be updated.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Loading times have been greatly improved.  It’s over twice as fast to load into the match on PS4 and Xbox One!</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Loading content before matchmaking now completes quicker.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Greatly reduced hitching when garbage collecting memory every minute.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Greatly reduced hitching caused by updating objects when the time of day changes from day to night, and vice-versa.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Reduced the amount of system and GPU memory used.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Optimized the visual effects played when distant buildings are hit.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Improved overall frame rate by optimizing how player animation and footsteps are handled.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Cozy Campfire and Boogie Bomb items no longer cause a hitch when seen the first time in a match.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Encountering players with specific skins for the first time in a match no longer causes a hitch.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span meshes. This also improves overall frame rate and reduces visual popping as you approach the trees.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<div dir=\"ltr\"><em><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></em></div>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li Pony\" animation so the character&#39;s arm no longer pops.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Players will no longer appear as if they are still holding a weapon after being hit special effects are now visible on low and medium settings.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"color:#b83df2;\">Audio</span></h2>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div As a result abilities will now correctly stagger, stun, and knockback enemies at high levels.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue where proximity mines wouldn’t disappear when the player who placed them left the match or died.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue where frag grenades could still be used even when the player didn’t have enough stamina to use it.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue where the Soldier&#39;s “Advanced Tactics” health bonus wasn’t properly  scaling in the late game.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue where the Frag Grenade perk “Cluster Bomb” was triggering twice rather than just once.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed the tool-tip for Air Strike which incorrectly stated that Air Strike drops 12 bombs, instead of 13.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue where the Outlander Fragment abilities TEDDY and Shock Tower weren’t receiving the energy damage bonus from the Energized support perk.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"color:#b83df2;\">UI</span></h2>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">The Commander XP curve has been inflated to make way for front-end crafting. This is to ensure that low-value items (e.g. ammo) are worth at least 1 Commander XP when crafted in the main menus.</div>\n\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Commander XP will appear larger than it did previously, but the amount of Commander XP you have earned toward your next level has been preserved, and the time it takes to level up remains unchanged.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Increased players’ current Daily Bonus XP and current Boost XP reserves to match the new Commander XP scale.</div>\n\t\t</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Squad screens will no longer show health and shield as being buffed at all times. It will instead properly show the buff/debuff arrows on health and shield stats when previewing slotting.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<div dir=\"ltr\"><em><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></em></div>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed a localization issue in the Transform menu.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue where the game background would move while using a controller to view the mission details.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue which caused players to lose menu functionality after leaving a party.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed a Research skill tree node that was missing a prerequisite.</div>\n\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Now the Research Tier 3 Party Resistance node requires Party Tech or Resistance.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Fixed an issue where recent player lists weren’t populating immediately after a game.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"color:#b83df2;\">Art/Animation</span></h2>\n\n<div dir=\"ltr\"><em><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></em></div>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Corrected flame animation rotation on the Lobber head.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 dir=\"ltr\"><span style=\"color:#b83df2;\">General</span></h2>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Searched chests and containers will no longer block players from building.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Cornstalks are no longer searchable.</div>\n\t</li>\n\t<li dir=\"ltr\">\n\t<div dir=\"ltr\">Your game window will now properly appear on the primary monitor.</div>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<div dir=\"ltr\"><em><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></em></div>\n\n<div dir=\"ltr\">\n<ul>\n\t<li>Fixed a rare crash on Xbox One.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<hr /><em>Experiencing issues updating, logging in or crashing in Fortnite? Watch the video for more info!</span></p>\n \n\n<div class=\"embed-responsive embed-responsive-16by9\"><iframe class=\"embed-responsive-item\" frameborder=\"0\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/Vs9X5vim3vo\" width=\"100%\"></iframe></div>\n\n<p dir=\"ltr\" style=\"line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;\"> </p>\n<br />\n ","featured":false,"date":"2017-12-14T17:00:00.000Z","link":"edbb55f8-f996-4b05-82c4-6ded406ff194","_id":"edbb55f8-f996-4b05-82c4-6ded406ff194","pageMapping":"edbb55f8-f996-4b05-82c4-6ded406ff194","slug":"fortnite-battle-royale-season-2-battle-pass-is-here","urlPattern":"/zh-HK/blog/fortnite-battle-royale-season-2-battle-pass-is-here","locale":"zh-HK","_script":"undefined","category":["announcements"],"tags":[],"catLocaleMap":{},"nextSlug":"small-shield-potion-update","prevSlug":"battle-pass-season-2","prevExtLink":"/battle-pass/season-2"},{"trending":true,"noTopImage":false,"image":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2FBattle-pass%2FBattle-Pass_Header_1920x480-1920x480-9e44186463cbc27aacfcbc8c899df5bcc1921720.jpg","author":"The Fortnite Team","enableLightbox":false,"_type":"Common Post","shareImage":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2FBattle-pass%2FBattle-Pass_Header_1920x480-1920x480-9e44186463cbc27aacfcbc8c899df5bcc1921720.jpg","title":"Battle Pass is here!","content":"Play Battle Royale. Level up. Unlock Epic loot. Buy the Battle Pass to get cosmetic loot now. Then earn or buy even more rewards.","trendingImage":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2FBattle-pass%2FBattle-Pass_Header_1920x480-1920x480-9e44186463cbc27aacfcbc8c899df5bcc1921720.jpg","highlightImage":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2FBattle-pass%2FBattle-Pass_Header_1920x480-1920x480-9e44186463cbc27aacfcbc8c899df5bcc1921720.jpg","cat":"Announcements","sticky":false,"short":"Play Battle Royale. Level up. Unlock Epic loot. Buy the Battle Pass to get cosmetic loot now. Then earn or buy even more rewards.","featured":true,"externalLink":"/battle-pass/season-2","date":"2017-12-14T11:00:00.000Z","link":"7a931849-2505-4f70-b662-618c92492c77","_id":"7a931849-2505-4f70-b662-618c92492c77","pageMapping":"7a931849-2505-4f70-b662-618c92492c77","slug":"battle-pass-season-2","urlPattern":"/zh-HK/blog/battle-pass-season-2","locale":"zh-HK","_script":"undefined","category":["announcements"],"tags":[],"catLocaleMap":{},"nextSlug":"fortnite-battle-royale-season-2-battle-pass-is-here","prevSlug":"v1-11-patch-notes"}],"categoryTotals":{"patch notes":33,"announcements":43,"補丁說明":1,"community":5,"announcement":2,"patches":1,"events":1,"announcments":1,"all":87},"topFeatured":[{"trending":true,"noTopImage":false,"image":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fservice-updates-and-call-to-action%2F480_blog-1920x480-8d36feeac3c5284983bbb2ac51a05aaf354c2c8b.jpg","author":"The Epic Team","enableLightbox":false,"_type":"Common Post","shareImage":"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fservice-updates-and-call-to-action%2FBlog_02-1920x1080-8465be714d0d9c27e74562a4a49c42a467fe9e25.jpg","title":"Postmortem of Service Outage at 3.4M CCU","content":"Fortnite hit a new peak of <strong>3.4 million concurrent players</strong> last Sunday… and that didn’t come without issues!  This blog post aims to share technical details about the challenges of rapidly scaling a game and its online services far beyond our wildest growth expectations.<br />\n<br />\n<strong>Also, Epic Games needs YOU!</strong>  If you have domain expertise to solve problems like these, and you’d like to contribute to Fortnite and other efforts, join Epic in <strong>Seattle</strong>, <strong>North Carolina</strong>, <strong>Salt Lake City</strong>, <strong>San Francisco</strong>, <strong>UK</strong>, <strong>Stockholm</strong>, <strong>Seoul</strong>, or elsewhere!  Please shoot us an email at <strong>OnlineJobs@epicgames.com</strong>.\n<h2>Postmortem of February 3rd and 4th outages</h2>\n<br />\nThe extreme load caused 6 different incidents between Saturday and Sunday, with a mix of partial and total service disruptions to Fortnite.\n<h3><strong>MCP database latency</strong></h3>\nFortnite has a service called MCP (remember the Tron nemesis?) which players contact in order to retrieve game profiles, statistics, items, matchmaking info and more. It’s backed by several sets of databases used to persistently store this data. The Fortnite game service is our largest database to date.<br />\n<br />\nThe primary MCP database is comprised of 9 MongoDB shards, where each shard has a writer, two read replicas, and a hidden replica for redundancy. At a high level user specific data is spread across 8 shards, whereas the remaining shard contains matchmaking sessions, shared service caches, and runtime configuration data.<br />\n<br />\nThe MCP is architected such that each service has a db connection pool to a sidecar process that in turn maintains a connection pool to all of our shards. At peak the MCP handles 124k client requests per second, which translates to 318k database reads and 132k database writes per second with a sub 10ms average database response time. Of that, matchmaking requests account for roughly 15% of all db queries and 11% of all writes across a single shard. In addition our current matchmaking implementation requires data to be in a single collection.<br />\n<br />\nAt peak we see an issue where the matchmaking shard begins queuing writes waiting on available writer resources. This can cause db update times to spike in the 40k+ ms range per operation causing MCP threads to block. Players experience unusually long wait times not just attempting to matchmake, but with all operations.  We have investigated this in detail and it is currently unclear to us and support why our writes are being queued in this way but we are working towards a root cause.<br />\n<br />\nThis issue does not recover and the db process soon becomes unresponsive, at which point we need to perform a manual primary failover in order to restore functionality. During these outages this procedure was being repeated multiple times per hour. Each failover causing a brief window of matchmaking instability followed by recovery.\n<h3><strong>MCP thread configuration</strong></h3>\nPrior to the launch of Fortnite, we had made a change to the packaging of the MCP. As part of that we introduced a bug limiting the number of available service threads below what we considered to be a safe default for our scale at the time. As part of a recent performance pass, this mistake was corrected by reverting it to our previous intended value.<br />\n<br />\nHowever once deployed to our live environment, we noticed requests experiencing increased latency (double ms average to double seconds) that was not present in our pre-production environments. This was diagnosed as db connection pool starvation via real-time cpu sampling through a diagnostics endpoint. In order to quickly remediate the issue we rolled back to our previous thread pool configuration.<br />\n<br />\nWhat we expected to be a performance improvement resulted in the opposite and was only revealed at peak production workloads. <br />\n<br />\nThe above MCP issues on Saturday can be seen here, with spikes partially representing matchmaking db failures and overall poor performance due to db thread pool starvation and a gradual rolling deploy.<br />\n<br />\n<img alt=\"pasted-image-0-(5).png\" height=\"auto\" src=\"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fpostmortem-of-service-outage-at-3-4m-ccu%2Fpasted-image-0-%285%29-785x424-e0866560ae6dc03bca28113899866a9ff66090a3.png\" width=\"auto\" /><br />\n<br />\nThe impact of just matchmaking db failures on Sunday can be seen below:<br />\n<br />\n<img alt=\"pasted-image-0-(1).png\" height=\"auto\" src=\"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fpostmortem-of-service-outage-at-3-4m-ccu%2Fpasted-image-0-%281%29-789x421-e61a38ac93a6f9646d33a0da6d0fcfacb290df50.png\" width=\"auto\" />\n<h3><strong>Account Service outage</strong></h3>\nAccount Service is the core Epic service which maintains user account data and serves as an authentication endpoint. Service in numbers:\n\n<ul style=\"margin-left: 40px;\">\n\t<li>Throughput: 40k - 100k req/sec (2.5M - 6M rpm). Up to 160k/sec at land rush.</li>\n\t<li>Latency:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>All APIs: avg < 10ms, p99 < 100ms, p99.9 < 400ms</li>\n\t\t<li>Sign In: avg < 100ms</li>\n\t\t<li>Auth check: avg < 5ms</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li>Sign up: 1k - 3k a minute.</li>\n\t<li>Sign in/out: 0.5k - 1k fresh sign ins /sec . Plus 0.7k - 1.5k refreshes /sec (session extension).</li>\n</ul>\n<br />\nAccount Service is a complex application with a JAXRS-based web-service component and a number of sidecar processes, one of which is an Nginx proxy sitting in front of it.<br />\n<br />\n<img alt=\"0_0.png\" height=\"auto\" src=\"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fpostmortem-of-service-outage-at-3-4m-ccu%2F0_0-1600x883-feeb5a4593170bcaee886082bd6e61477b552e98.png\" width=\"auto\" /><br />\nThe main purpose of this proxy is to shortcut an access token verification path. All traffic is routed through this proxy, but only access token verification traffic is checked against cache as shown above. With all other calls simply passing through to the main application.<br />\n<br />\nOn Sunday, there was an incident when Memcached instability saturated Nginx capacity (essentially, occupied all available worker threads), so that other traffic simply couldn’t get through to the main application.<br />\n<br />\n<img alt=\"pasted-image-0-(2).png\" height=\"auto\" src=\"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fpostmortem-of-service-outage-at-3-4m-ccu%2Fpasted-image-0-%282%29-1600x1035-0a90eae9762b19a57a66b732521b9917dbf2ff38.png\" width=\"auto\" /><br />\n<br />\nBelow is a quick post-mortem summary:\n<ul style=\"margin-left: 40px;\">\n\t<li>Timeline:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>2018-02-04 18:30 UTC - 2018-02-04 20:20 UTC</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li>Root cause:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Nginx in front of the Java application was saturated, and traffic was limited to the application. Hence all our JVM-level protection from situations like this didn’t help.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li>Incident Details:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Our memcached component started failing under the load due to network and connection saturation.</li>\n\t\t<li>Nginx was next in line and got stuck on timing out Memcached calls (100ms) quickly running out of free worker threads and becoming unable to serve other traffic. Including health-check calls.</li>\n\t\t<li>All the verify calls have fallen through to JVM layer with added +100ms memcached timeouts and added to Redis load.</li>\n\t\t<li>Missed health check requests caused the load balancer to pull all the nodes out of rotation effectively imposing full service downtime.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li>Impact:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Good news though is that this had moderate impact on players in match due to resiliency measures we have in place.</li>\n\t\t<li>Signing in (and out) was mostly blocked and our Epic Games Launcher would sign players out with an error.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li>Next steps:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Leveraging Level 7 routing in ALB to direct all non-verify traffic directly to our Java application, which in turn has a number of protection measures implemented against saturation like this.</li>\n\t\t<li>Significantly increasing Memcached capacity.</li>\n\t\t<li>Followed by removing Nginx + Memcached couple altogether out of equation.</li>\n\t\t<li>We still have a lot of exciting problems to solve. Problems like implementing effective sharding of persistent data with pretty complex set of secondary indices we have to maintain.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3><strong>XMPP outage</strong></h3>\nBeing a foundation for online presence, text messaging and a number of other social features like parties, XMPP Service plays a significant role in delivering quality social experience to our players. This makes all XMPP service instabilities immediately visible to our community.<br />\n<br />\nXMPP Service is an Instant Messaging solution customized to support a subset of <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XMPP\">XMPP protocol</a> and protocol extensions according to platform needs.<br />\n<br />\nXMPP Service in numbers:\n<ul style=\"margin-left: 40px;\">\n\t<li>Online connections: way over 3 Million ++</li>\n\t<li>Throughput in packets:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Total: ~600k / sec (including aux traffic, forwarding and broadcast effect).</li>\n\t\t<li>Presences: ~180k / sec</li>\n\t\t<li>Notification: ~50k / sec</li>\n\t\t<li>Messages: ~40k / sec</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\nWe leverage XMPP for the following features:\n\n<ul style=\"margin-left: 40px;\">\n\t<li>Online presence</li>\n\t<li>Push notifications</li>\n\t<li>Whispers </li>\n\t<li>Group chat - for parties, for team chat and global rooms.</li>\n</ul>\n<br />\nIn its essence XMPP, as majority of other instant messaging services, is a highly async pub-sub system pumping packets - messages, presences, commands and various aux data - through the cluster from a sender to an addressee (or a set of).<br />\n<br />\nXMPP supports multiple end-user connection protocols. Our service uses two: TCP and WebSockets. We maintain millions of persistent and relatively long living TCP connections from clients concurrently. This comes at a cost of system complexity, as this case significantly differs from our typical RESTful web services.<br />\n<br />\nEpic XMPP is one component in a family of Social web-services. It depends on other services including <strong>Friends Service</strong>, which supplies XMPP with friends information. We use this information to enable presence flow between players.<br />\n<br />\nOn Sunday we had a situation while mitigating a known instability problem that resulted in overloading a downstream system component and effectively paralyzing presence flow.  Without presence, a user who is your friend cannot see that you are online, breaking most of our social features including the ability to form parties.<br />\n<br />\nGraphs below:\n<ul style=\"margin-left: 40px;\">\n\t<li>At the top - instability and connection migration from Blue cluster to Green cluster (time in UTC).</li>\n\t<li>On the left - calls made by stand-by XMPP cluster to Friends Service. XMPP perspective.</li>\n\t<li>On the right - traffic handled by Friends load balancer. Once recovered, it was able to handle all queued traffic.</li>\n</ul>\n<img alt=\"pasted-image-0-(6)_640x198_1518103087134.png\" height=\"auto\" src=\"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fpostmortem-of-service-outage-at-3-4m-ccu%2Fpasted-image-0-%286%29_640x198_1518103087134-640x198-4c5ef526c4c3d0236ae9fa00f0553185e63aa834.png\" width=\"auto\" /><br />\n<img alt=\"pasted-image-0-(7)_640x200_1518103097086.png\" height=\"auto\" src=\"https://cdn2.unrealengine.com/Fortnite%2Fblog%2Fpostmortem-of-service-outage-at-3-4m-ccu%2Fpasted-image-0-%287%29_640x200_1518103097086-640x200-79d303eb5cefaa35e2d67bf213d059b39b936e42.png\" width=\"auto\" /><br />\n<br />\nHere is a quick summary of the incident:\n<ul style=\"margin-left: 40px;\">\n\t<li>Timeline:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>2018-02-04 22:00 UTC - 2018-02-05 00:15 UTC</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li>Root cause:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Friends Service internal load balancer - the one on critical path for XMPP - got overloaded and pushed into an error state.</li>\n\t\t<li>ELB could not quickly recover due to specifics of failover process and outdated network configuration - ELB subnet was short on free IPs to provision replacement.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li>Incident Details:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Due to a recently introduced memory leak, XMPP was on a monitored path to falling into unstable state.</li>\n\t\t<li>We planned to replace it with another ready and stand-by cluster with the leak already fixed.</li>\n\t\t<li>We expected cluster to survive through weekend, so that we could schedule a proper maintenance during working week days.</li>\n\t\t<li>Unfortunately, Game Services and Account Service instability significantly increased the effect of the leak. And at 22:00 UTC on Sunday we started losing cluster nodes and disconnecting players.</li>\n\t\t<li>A decision was made to immediately failover to a stand-by cluster via green/blue deployment strategy, when we instantly flip all the traffic to another set of endpoints.</li>\n\t\t<li>Unfortunately, landrush of reconnecting people at the time has effectively killed one of the <strong>Friends Service</strong> load balancers paralyzing our ability to setup presence flow on new connections.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li>Impact:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>As a result, though people did actually connect to XMPP, the UI showed everyone as offline due to missing presence flow.</li>\n\t\t<li>Effectively, a “dark room” situation.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n\t<li>Next steps:\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>We’re in a process of upgrading load-balancer solution for Friends Service and other platform services to address issues like above.</li>\n\t\t<li>We’re fixing our VPC configuration to ensure subnet capacity.</li>\n\t\t<li>There are also longer-term problems team is actively working on. For example with current architecture XMPP cluster represents a full mesh. Each cluster node is connected to each other. With 10 connections between each node and 101 nodes in cluster it effectively spends 1k sockets per node just on cluster connections.</li>\n\t\t<li>Each XMPP node can hold only up to N connections with current solution. Hence there is a theoretical limit on optimal number of cluster nodes (and hence CCU capacity) we can maintain without solution redesign.</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3><strong>Cloud capacity limits and throttling</strong></h3>\nWe run Fortnite’s dedicated game servers primarily on thousands of c4.8xlarge AWS instances, which scale up and down with our daily peak of players.  This means our count of instances is always fluctuating and nonlinear in growth.<br />\n<br />\nWhile capacity limits caused no disruption to the game, we had to react quickly to adjust some of our services limits. Fortunately our monitoring alerted us quickly and we were able to make the necessary changes.  The limit we hit was the total instance limit in the region, which would affect our ability to scale our services in the entire region. We have also hit several API rate limits and we cover our corrective actions in the next steps section.\n<h3><strong>Available IP exhaustion</strong></h3>\nWe run in multiple availability zones in cloud providers for our core services and our standard subnets are /24 giving us 251 usable IPs per subnet.  Multiple factors such as shared subnets, instance changes and scaling across many services caused us to run out of IPs.  While we were able to shift many components without any interruption, due to other events described above, it caused extended load balancer recovery times.\n\n<h2>Next Steps and Updates</h2>\n<br />\nOur top focus right now is to ensure service availability. Our next steps are below:<br />\n \n<ul style=\"margin-left: 40px;\">\n\t<li><strong>Identify and resolve the root cause of our DB performance issues.</strong> We’ve flown Mongo experts on-site to analyze our DB and usage, as well as provide real-time support during heavy load on weekends.</li>\n\t<li><strong>Optimize, reduce, and eliminate all unnecessary calls to the backend from the client or servers. </strong>Some examples are periodically verifying user entitlements when this is already happening implicitly with each game service call. Registering and unregistering individual players on a game play session when these calls can be done more efficiently in bulk, Deferring XMPP connections to avoid thrashing during login/logout scenarios. Social features recovering quickly from ELB or other connectivity issues.  When 3.4 million clients are connected at the same time these inefficiencies add up quickly.</li>\n\t<li><strong>Optimize how we store the matchmaking session data in our DB.</strong> Even without a root cause for the current write queue issue we can improve performance by changing how we store this ephemeral data. We’re prototyping in-memory database solutions that may be more suited to this use case, and looking at how we can restructure our current data in order to make it properly shardable.</li>\n\t<li><strong>Improve our internal operation excellence focus in our production and development process. </strong>This includes building new tools to compare API call patterns between builds, setting up focused weekly reviews of performance, expanding our monitoring and alerting systems, and continually improving our post-mortem processes.</li>\n\t<li><strong>Improve our alerting and monitoring of known cloud provider limits, and subnet IP utilization.</strong></li>\n\t<li><strong>Reducing blast radius during incidents.</strong>  A number of our core services are globally impacting to all players.  While we operate game servers all over the world, expanding to additional cloud providers and supporting core services in multiple geographical locations will help reduce player impact when services fail.  Expanding our footprint also increases our operational overhead and complexity.  If you have experience in running large worldwide multi cloud services and/or infrastructure we would love to hear from you.</li>\n\t<li><strong>Rearchitecting our core messaging stack.</strong>  Our stack wasn’t architected to handle this scale and we need to look at larger changes in our architecture to support our growth.</li>\n\t<li><strong>Digging deeper into our data and DB storage.</strong>  We hit new and interesting limits as our services grow and our data sets and usage patterns grow larger and larger every day.  We’re looking for experienced DBAs to join our team and help us solve some of the scaling bottlenecks we run into as our games grow.</li>\n\t<li><strong>Scaling our internal infrastructure.</strong>  When our game services grow in size so do our internal monitoring, metrics, and logging along with other internal needs.  As our footprint expands our needs for more advanced deployment, configuration tooling and infrastructure also increases.  If you have experience scaling and improving internal systems and are interested in what is going on here at Epic, let’s have a chat.</li>\n\t<li><strong>Performance at scale. </strong> Along with a number of things mentioned, even small performance changes over N nodes collectively make large impacts for our services and player experience.  If you have experience with large scale performance tuning and want to come make improvements that directly impact players please reach out to us.</li>\n\t<li><strong>MCP Re-architecture</strong>\n\t<ul>\n\t\t<li>Move specific functionality out of MCP to microservices</li>\n\t\t<li>Event sourcing data models for user data</li>\n\t\t<li>Actor based modeling of user sessions</li>\n\t</ul>\n\t</li>\n</ul>\n<br />\nProblems that affect service availability are our primary focus above all else right now. We want you all to know we take these outages very seriously, conducting in-depth post-mortems on each incident to identify the root cause and decide on the best plan of action.   The online team has been working diligently over the past month to keep up with the demand created by the rapid week-over-week growth of our user base.<br />\n<br />\nWhile we cannot promise there won’t be future outages as our services reach new peaks, we hope to live by this great quote from Futurama, “<strong>When you do things right, people won&#39;t be sure you&#39;ve done anything at all.</strong>”\n\n<h2>Remember, we need you!</h2>\n<br />\nIt’s been an amazing and exhilarating experience to grow Fortnite from our previous peak of 60K concurrent players to 3.4M in just a few months, making it perhaps the <strong>biggest PC/console game in the world</strong>!  All of this has been accomplished in just a few months by a small team of veteran online developers -- and we’d love to welcome a few more folks like yourself to join Epic Games on this journey!<br />\n<br />\n<strong>So, please contact us at OnlineJobs@epicgames.com, and join one of Epic’s high-quality development offices around the world!</strong><br ","sticky":false,"short":"A technical update on our recent service issues  at 3.4M CCU, including a call to
